# Gemini Character Generation Prompts

300 prompts for Nano Banana 2 (gemini-2.5-flash-image). Paste each into gemini.google.com.

Save each image as `gemini_NNN.png` into `/Volumes/TAMWoolff/data/raw/gemini_diverse/`.

---

<!-- ## Batch 4: Prompts 301-400 — User-Input-Aligned

These prompts target the characters Strata users most commonly bring to the app: indie game sprites, VTuber avatars, D&D/TTRPG art, visual novel sprites, gacha/mobile game characters, webcomic OCs, and modern casual outfits. They also fill training gaps in the segmentation model (loose clothing vs body, hair occlusion, accessories, chibi proportions) and joint model (foreshortened limbs, crossed arms, seated poses users try to rig).

## Batch 5: Pose & View Diversity (1001-1300)

Focus: back views, three-quarter back, sitting, kneeling, arms raised, dynamic action, crouching, leaning. The model needs pose diversity more than style diversity at this point.
